## In this file, lines starting with # are comments.  The lines starting
## with ## are meant solely as comments, whereas the lines starting with
## only # are followed by example entries.

## If the "-c" option indicates that your host name is wrong,
## start a line with "N web" followed by the name for this server,
## similar to the next line.
#N this.server.name.org

## If you are required to go through a proxy server to connect to the
## Internet, start a line with "P " then specify the proxy server name
## and port number separated by a colon, as shown in the next line
#P tothenet.mylib.org:6588www.jstage.jst.go.jp

## As distributed, the only database available is AltaVista
## (for testing purposes).  In general, this file contains one
## character options of T (title), U HTTPHeader X

#NeverProxy oecd.metastore.ingenta.com(URL) and D (domain).  For
## each database, you start with a T (title) line llmccontaining a
## title to display in the menu, a U (URL) line for the main entry
## URL for your site, and one or more D (domain) lines specifying the
## domains used by the database vendor.
##
## This file contains examples for main common database vendors.  To
## enable a specific vendor, remove the # from the beginning of eachsciencedirect.com
## line, and customize the T (title) and U (URL) as appropriate.

## Databases begin
